<summary>🔧 Tool: Write -- `validation.ts`</summary>

**Input:**

**File:** `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/validation.ts`  

```
/**
 * Shared validation utilities for API route parameter validation.
 */

const UUID_RE = /^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{12}$/i

/**
 * Validates that a string is a valid UUID v4 format.
 * Used for path parameter validation to prevent path traversal and invalid lookups.
 */
export function isValidUuid(id: string): boolean {
  return UUID_RE.test(id)
}

```

**Result:**

File created successfully at: /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/validation.ts

**Input:**

*Wait 30s then check agent completion status*  

```bash
sleep 30 && echo "Checking agent completion..." && for f in /private/tmp/claude-501/-Users-emanuelesabetta-ai-maestro/tasks/a{6f1c1e,6d3ae7,9a49a8,0eac85,e581dd,0df560,f77936,241cd7,192d28,0f0fb8,a28290,63fbc4,4efeb5,02c674,c0c48a,77be1c,aacfa1,97029d,e8a445}.output; do name=$(basename "$f" .output); last=$(tail -1 "$f" 2>/dev/null); if echo "$last" | grep -q '"type":"result"'; then echo "$name: DONE"; elif echo "$last" | grep -q 'DONE\|FAILED'; then echo "$name: DONE"; else echo "$name: RUNNING"; fi; done
```

     1→/**  
     2→ * Transfer Registry — manages team transfer requests  
     3→ *  
     4→ * When a COS or MANAGER tries to move an agent from a closed team  
     5→ * led by a different COS, a transfer request is created that must  
     6→ * be approved by the source team's COS before the move takes effect.  
     7→ */

    13→import type { TransferRequest, TransfersFile } from '@/types/governance'

    15→  
    16→const AIMAESTRO_DIR = path.join(os.homedir(), '.aimaestro')  
    17→const TRANSFERS_FILE = path.join(AIMAESTRO_DIR, 'governance-transfers.json')  
    18→  
    19→function ensureDir(): void {  
    20→  if (!existsSync(AIMAESTRO_DIR)) {  
    21→    mkdirSync(AIMAESTRO_DIR, { recursive: true })  
    22→  }  
    23→}  
    24→  
    25→/** Load all transfer requests from disk */  
    26→export function loadTransfers(): TransferRequest[] {  
    27→  ensureDir()  
    28→  if (!existsSync(TRANSFERS_FILE)) {  
    29→    return []  
    30→  }  
    31→  try {  
    32→    const raw = readFileSync(TRANSFERS_FILE, 'utf-8')  
    33→    const data: TransfersFile = JSON.parse(raw)  
    34→    return data.requests || []  
    35→  } catch {  
    36→    return []  
    37→  }  
    38→}  
    39→

    43→  const data: TransfersFile = { version: 1, requests }

Fix all issues in /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/message-send.ts:  

1. SHOULD-FIX: `generateMessageId()` (~line 57-59) uses `Math.random()`. The `crypto` module is already imported. Replace with:  
```typescript
function generateMessageId(): string {
  const timestamp = Date.now()
  const random = crypto.randomBytes(6).toString('hex')
  return `msg-${timestamp}-${random}`
}
```
If `crypto` is imported as Node's crypto module, use it. If not, add the import.  

2. SHOULD-FIX: `forwardFromUI()` (~line 426-453) does not set `fromLabel` or `toLabel` on the forwarded message. Add these fields to the forwardedMessage object:  
```typescript
fromLabel: fromResolved.displayName || fromResolved.alias,
toLabel: toResolved.displayName || toResolved.alias,
```

3. SHOULD-FIX: `buildAMPEnvelope` (~line 88) uses `message.amp?.signature || ''`. For unsigned messages, use `'unsigned'` instead of empty string so downstream can distinguish:  
```typescript
signature: message.amp?.signature || 'unsigned',
```

4. NIT: `parseQualifiedName` (~line 46-51) doesn't handle multiple `@` signs robustly. Use `indexOf` + `substring` instead of `split`:  
```typescript
function parseQualifiedName(qualifiedName: string): { identifier: string; hostId: string | null } {
  const atIndex = qualifiedName.indexOf('@')
  if (atIndex > 0 && atIndex < qualifiedName.length - 1) {
    return { identifier: qualifiedName.substring(0, atIndex), hostId: qualifiedName.substring(atIndex + 1) }
  }
  return { identifier: qualifiedName, hostId: null }
}
```

```
  const parts = qualifiedName.split('@')
```

**New:**  
```
function parseQualifiedName(qualifiedName: string): { identifier: string; hostId: string | null } {
  // Use indexOf instead of split to handle multiple '@' signs robustly
  const atIndex = qualifiedName.indexOf('@')
  if (atIndex > 0 && atIndex < qualifiedName.length - 1) {
    return { identifier: qualifiedName.substring(0, atIndex), hostId: qualifiedName.substring(atIndex + 1) }
  }
  return { identifier: qualifiedName, hostId: null }
}
```

<summary>🔧 Tool: Read -- `file-lock.ts`</summary>

```json
  "file_path": "/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/file-lock.ts"

```

**Result:**

     1→/**  
     2→ * File Lock — in-process mutex for serializing load→modify→save operations  
     3→ *  
     4→ * Prevents concurrent read-modify-write races within a single Node.js process.  
     5→ * Each registry file gets its own named lock. When one API request is mid-write,  
     6→ * other requests for the same file queue up and run sequentially.  
     7→ *  
     8→ * This is sufficient for Phase 1 (single Next.js process, localhost).  
     9→ * For multi-process deployments, replace with advisory file locks (e.g., proper-lockfile).  
    10→ */  
    11→  
    12→// Map of lock name -> queue of pending resolve callbacks  
    13→const locks = new Map<string, Array<() => void>>()  
    14→// Set of currently held lock names  
    15→const held = new Set<string>()  
    16→  
    17→/**  
    18→ * Acquire a named lock. Returns a release function.  
    19→ * If the lock is already held, the caller awaits until it is released.  
    20→ */  
    21→export function acquireLock(name: string): Promise<() => void> {  
    22→  if (!held.has(name)) {  
    23→    // Lock is free — acquire immediately  
    24→    held.add(name)  
    25→    return Promise.resolve(() => releaseLock(name))  
    26→  }  
    27→  
    28→  // Lock is held — enqueue and wait  
    29→  return new Promise<() => void>((resolve) => {  
    30→    if (!locks.has(name)) {  
    31→      locks.set(name, [])  
    32→    }  
    33→    locks.get(name)!.push(() => {  
    34→      resolve(() => releaseLock(name))  
    35→    })  
    36→  })  
    37→}  
    38→  
    39→/**  
    40→ * Release a named lock and wake the next waiter if any.  
    41→ */  
    42→function releaseLock(name: string): void {  
    43→  const queue = locks.get(name)  
    44→  if (queue && queue.length > 0) {  
    45→    // Hand lock to next waiter (don't remove from held set)  
    46→    const next = queue.shift()!  
    47→    if (queue.length === 0) {  
    48→      locks.delete(name)  
    49→    }  
    50→    next()  
    51→  } else {  
    52→    // No waiters — release the lock  
    53→    hel  

... [473 more chars truncated]  

</details>

   102→}

   104→export function deleteDocument(teamId: string, docId: string): boolean {  
   105→  const documents = loadDocuments(teamId)  
   106→  const filtered = documents.filter(d => d.id !== docId)  
   107→  if (filtered.length === documents.length) return false  
   108→  saveDocuments(teamId, filtered)  
   109→  return true

    60→/**  
    61→ * Resolve task dependencies and compute derived fields  
    62→ */  
    63→export function resolveTaskDeps(tasks: Task[]): TaskWithDeps[] {  
    64→  // loadAgents() has internal caching (_cachedAgents), so repeated calls are cheap  
    65→  const agents = loadAgents()  
    66→  const taskMap = new Map(tasks.map(t => [t.id, t]))  
    67→  
    68→  return tasks.map(task => {  
    69→    // Compute blocks (reverse of blockedBy)  
    70→    const blocks = tasks  
    71→      .filter(t => t.blockedBy.includes(task.id))  
    72→      .map(t => t.id)  
    73→  
    74→    // Compute isBlocked  
    75→    const isBlocked = task.blockedBy.some(depId => {  
    76→      const dep = taskMap.get(depId)  
    77→      return dep && dep.status !== 'completed'  
    78→    })  
    79→  
    80→    // Resolve assignee name  
    81→    let assigneeName: string | undefined  
    82→    if (task.assigneeAgentId) {  
    83→      const agent = agents.find(a => a.id === task.assigneeAgentId)  
    84→      if (agent) {  
    85→        assigneeName = agent.label || agent.name || agent.alias || agent.id.slice(0, 8)  
    86→      }  
    87→    }  
    88→  
    89→    return {  
    90→      ...task,  
    91→      blocks,  
    92→      isBlocked,  
    93→      assigneeName,  
    94→    }  
    95→  })  
    96→}

   138→export function updateTask(  
   139→  teamId: string,  
   140→  taskId: string,  
   141→  updates: Partial<Pick<Task, 'subject' | 'description' | 'status' | 'assigneeAgentId' | 'blockedBy' | 'priority'>>  
   142→): Promise<{ task: Task | null; unblocked: Task[] }> {  
   143→  return withLock('tasks-' + teamId, () => {  
   144→    const tasks = loadTasks(teamId)  
   145→    const index = tasks.findIndex(t => t.id === taskId)  
   146→    if (index === -1) return { task: null, unblocked: [] }  
   147→  
   148→    const now = new Date().toISOString()  
   149→    const wasCompleted = tasks[index].status === 'completed'  
   150→    const isNowCompleted = updates.status === 'completed'  
   151→  
   152→    tasks[index] = {  
   153→      ...tasks[index],  
   154→      ...updates,  
   155→      updatedAt: now,  
   156→    }  
   157→  
   158→    // Set timestamps based on status changes  
   159→    if ((updates.status === 'in_progress' || updates.status === 'review') && !tasks[index].startedAt) {  
   160→      tasks[index].startedAt = now  
   161→    }  
   162→    if (updates.status === 'completed' && !tasks[index].completedAt) {  
   163→      tasks[index].completedAt = now  
   164→    }  
   165→  
   166→    // Clear timestamps when moving backward in workflow  
   167→    if (updates.status && updates.status !== 'completed') {  
   168→      tasks[index].completedAt = undefined  
   169→    }  
   170→    if (updates.status && (updates.status === 'backlog' || updates.status === 'pending')) {  
   171→      tasks[index].startedAt = undefined  
   172→    }  
   173→  
   174→    // Find newly unblocked tasks when a task is completed  
   175→    let unblocked: Task[] = []  
   176→    if (!wasCompleted && isNowCompleted) {  
   177→      unblocked = tasks.filter(t => {  
   178→        if (!t.blockedBy.includes(taskId)) return false  
   179→        // Check if ALL blockers are now completed  
   180→        return t.blockedBy.every(depId => {  
   181→          const dep = tasks.find(d => d.id === depId)  
   182→          ret  

... [493 more chars truncated]

**Old:**  
```
export function createDocument(data: {
  teamId: string
  title: string
  content: string
  pinned?: boolean
  tags?: string[]
}): TeamDocument {
  const documents = loadDocuments(data.teamId)
  const now = new Date().toISOString()

  const doc: TeamDocument = {
    id: uuidv4(),
    teamId: data.teamId,
    title: data.title,
    content: data.content,
    pinned: data.pinned || false,
    tags: data.tags || [],
    createdAt: now,
    updatedAt: now,
  }

  documents.push(doc)
  saveDocuments(data.teamId, documents)
  return doc
}
```

**New:**  
```
export function createDocument(data: {
  teamId: string
  title: string
  content: string
  pinned?: boolean
  tags?: string[]
}): Promise<TeamDocument> {
  return withLock('documents-' + data.teamId, () => {
    const documents = loadDocuments(data.teamId)
    const now = new Date().toISOString()

    const doc: TeamDocument = {
      id: uuidv4(),
      teamId: data.teamId,
      title: data.title,
      content: data.content,
      pinned: data.pinned || false,
      tags: data.tags || [],
      createdAt: now,
      updatedAt: now,
    }

    documents.push(doc)
    saveDocuments(data.teamId, documents)
    return doc
  })
}
```

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-19 17:49:17]*

<summary>🔧 Tool: Edit -- `document-registry.ts`</summary>

**Input:**

**Old:**  
```
export function updateDocument(
  teamId: string,
  docId: string,
  updates: Partial<Pick<TeamDocument, 'title' | 'content' | 'pinned' | 'tags'>>
): TeamDocument | null {
  const documents = loadDocuments(teamId)
  const index = documents.findIndex(d => d.id === docId)
  if (index === -1) return null

  documents[index] = {
    ...documents[index],
    ...updates,
    updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  }

  saveDocuments(teamId, documents)
  return documents[index]
}
```

**New:**  
```
export function updateDocument(
  teamId: string,
  docId: string,
  updates: Partial<Pick<TeamDocument, 'title' | 'content' | 'pinned' | 'tags'>>
): Promise<TeamDocument | null> {
  return withLock('documents-' + teamId, () => {
    const documents = loadDocuments(teamId)
    const index = documents.findIndex(d => d.id === docId)
    if (index === -1) return null

    documents[index] = {
      ...documents[index],
      ...updates,
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    }

    saveDocuments(teamId, documents)
    return documents[index]
  })
}
```

**Result:**

The file /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/document-registry.ts has been updated successfully.

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-19 17:49:21]*

**Old:**  
```
export function deleteDocument(teamId: string, docId: string): boolean {
  const documents = loadDocuments(teamId)
  const filtered = documents.filter(d => d.id !== docId)
  if (filtered.length === documents.length) return false
  saveDocuments(teamId, filtered)
  return true
}
```

**New:**  
```
export function deleteDocument(teamId: string, docId: string): Promise<boolean> {
  return withLock('documents-' + teamId, () => {
    const documents = loadDocuments(teamId)
    const filtered = documents.filter(d => d.id !== docId)
    if (filtered.length === documents.length) return false
    saveDocuments(teamId, filtered)
    return true
  })
}
```

**Result:**

The file /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/document-registry.ts has been updated successfully.

**Result:**

     1→/**  
     2→ * Document Registry - File-based CRUD for team document persistence  
     3→ *  
     4→ * Storage: ~/.aimaestro/teams/docs-{teamId}.json (one per team)  
     5→ * Mirrors the pattern from lib/task-registry.ts  
     6→ */  
     7→  
     8→import fs from 'fs'  
     9→import path from 'path'  
    10→import os from 'os'  
    11→import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid'  
    12→import { withLock } from '@/lib/file-lock'  
    13→import type { TeamDocument, TeamDocumentsFile } from '@/types/document'  
    14→  
    15→const TEAMS_DIR = path.join(os.homedir(), '.aimaestro', 'teams')  
    16→  
    17→function ensureTeamsDir() {  
    18→  if (!fs.existsSync(TEAMS_DIR)) {  
    19→    fs.mkdirSync(TEAMS_DIR, { recursive: true })  
    20→  }  
    21→}  
    22→  
    23→function docsFilePath(teamId: string): string {  
    24→  return path.join(TEAMS_DIR, `docs-${teamId}.json`)  
    25→}  
    26→  
    27→export function loadDocuments(teamId: string): TeamDocument[] {  
    28→  try {  
    29→    ensureTeamsDir()  
    30→    const filePath = docsFilePath(teamId)  
    31→    if (!fs.existsSync(filePath)) {  
    32→      return []  
    33→    }  
    34→    const data = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8')  
    35→    const parsed: TeamDocumentsFile = JSON.parse(data)  
    36→    return Array.isArray(parsed.documents) ? parsed.documents : []  
    37→  } catch (error) {  
    38→    console.error(`Failed to load documents for team ${teamId}:`, error)  
    39→    return []  
    40→  }  
    41→}  
    42→  
    43→export function saveDocuments(teamId: string, documents: TeamDocument[]): boolean {  
    44→  try {  
    45→    ensureTeamsDir()  
    46→    const file: TeamDocumentsFile = { version: 1, documents }  
    47→    fs.writeFileSync(docsFilePath(teamId), JSON.stringify(file, null, 2), 'utf-8')  
    48→    return true  
    49→  } catch (error) {  
    50→    console.error(`Failed to save documents for team ${teamId}:`, error)  
    51→    return false  
    52→  }  
    53→}  
    54→  
    55→export function getDocument(teamId: string,  

... [2129 more chars truncated]

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-19 17:48:16]*

<details>
<summary>🔧 Tool: Read -- `file-lock.ts`</summary>

**Input:**

```json
{
  "file_path": "/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/file-lock.ts"
}
```

**Result:**

     1→/**  
     2→ * File Lock — in-process mutex for serializing load→modify→save operations  
     3→ *  
     4→ * Prevents concurrent read-modify-write races within a single Node.js process.  
     5→ * Each registry file gets its own named lock. When one API request is mid-write,  
     6→ * other requests for the same file queue up and run sequentially.  
     7→ *  
     8→ * This is sufficient for Phase 1 (single Next.js process, localhost).  
     9→ * For multi-process deployments, replace with advisory file locks (e.g., proper-lockfile).  
    10→ */  
    11→  
    12→// Map of lock name -> queue of pending resolve callbacks  
    13→const locks = new Map<string, Array<() => void>>()  
    14→// Set of currently held lock names  
    15→const held = new Set<string>()  
    16→  
    17→/**  
    18→ * Acquire a named lock. Returns a release function.  
    19→ * If the lock is already held, the caller awaits until it is released.  
    20→ */  
    21→export function acquireLock(name: string): Promise<() => void> {  
    22→  if (!held.has(name)) {  
    23→    // Lock is free — acquire immediately  
    24→    held.add(name)  
    25→    return Promise.resolve(() => releaseLock(name))  
    26→  }  
    27→  
    28→  // Lock is held — enqueue and wait  
    29→  return new Promise<() => void>((resolve) => {  
    30→    if (!locks.has(name)) {  
    31→      locks.set(name, [])  
    32→    }  
    33→    locks.get(name)!.push(() => {  
    34→      resolve(() => releaseLock(name))  
    35→    })  
    36→  })  
    37→}  
    38→  
    39→/**  
    40→ * Release a named lock and wake the next waiter if any.  
    41→ */  
    42→function releaseLock(name: string): void {  
    43→  const queue = locks.get(name)  
    44→  if (queue && queue.length > 0) {  
    45→    // Hand lock to next waiter (don't remove from held set)  
    46→    const next = queue.shift()!  
    47→    if (queue.length === 0) {  
    48→      locks.delete(name)  
    49→    }  
    50→    next()  
    51→  } else {  
    52→    // No waiters — release the lock  
    53→    hel  

... [473 more chars truncated]

     1→/**  
     2→ * Team Resource ACL — checks whether an agent (or web UI request)  
     3→ * is allowed to access a given team's resources.  
     4→ *  
     5→ * Open teams (type undefined or 'open') impose no restrictions.  
     6→ * Closed teams restrict access to the manager, chief-of-staff,  
     7→ * and team members only.  
     8→ */  
     9→  
    10→import { isManager } from './governance'  
    11→import { getTeam } from './team-registry'

    13→export interface TeamAccessInput {  
    14→  teamId: string  
    15→  requestingAgentId?: string // undefined = web UI request (always allowed)

    17→  
    18→export interface TeamAccessResult {  
    19→  allowed: boolean  
    20→  reason?: string  
    21→}  
    22→  
    23→/**  
    24→ * Determine whether the requester may access the team's resources.  
    25→ *  
    26→ * Decision order:  
    27→ *  1. Web UI (no agentId)      → allowed  
    28→ *  2. Team not found           → allowed (caller handles 404)  
    29→ *  3. Team is open / untyped   → allowed  
    30→ *  4. Requester is MANAGER     → allowed  
    31→ *  5. Requester is chief-of-staff → allowed  
    32→ *  6. Requester is a member    → allowed  
    33→ *  7. Otherwise                → denied  
    34→ */  
    35→export function checkTeamAccess(input: TeamAccessInput): TeamAccessResult {  
    36→  // 1. Web UI requests (no X-Agent-Id header) always pass.  
    37→  // KNOWN LIMITATION (Phase 1, localhost-only): Any local process that omits X-Agent-Id  
    38→  // gets full access, not just the web UI. Acceptable because Phase 1 runs on localhost  
    39→  // where all local processes are trusted.  
    40→  // TODO Phase 2: Add X-Request-Source header with per-session CSRF token to distinguish  
    41→  // genuine web UI requests from other local processes.  
    42→  if (input.requestingAgentId === undefined) {  
    43→    return { allowed: true }  
    44→  }  
    45→  
    46→  // 2. Team not found — let the caller deal with 404  
    47→  const team = getTeam(input.teamId)

     1→/**  
     2→ * File Lock — in-process mutex for serializing load→modify→save operations  
     3→ *  
     4→ * Prevents concurrent read-modify-write races within a single Node.js process.  
     5→ * Each registry file gets its own named lock. When one API request is mid-write,  
     6→ * other requests for the same file queue up and run sequentially.  
     7→ *  
     8→ * This is sufficient for Phase 1 (single Next.js process, localhost).  
     9→ * For multi-process deployments, replace with advisory file locks (e.g., proper-lockfile).

    11→  
    12→/**  
    13→ * LOCK ORDERING INVARIANT:  
    14→ * When acquiring multiple locks, always acquire in this order:  
    15→ *   1. 'teams'  
    16→ *   2. 'transfers'  
    17→ *   3. 'governance'  
    18→ * Violating this order will cause deadlock.

   117→function parseAMPAddress(address: string): {  
   118→  name: string  
   119→  tenant: string  
   120→  provider: string  
   121→  scope?: string  
   122→} | null {  
   123→  const atIndex = address.indexOf('@')  
   124→  if (atIndex === -1) return null  
   125→  
   126→  const name = address.substring(0, atIndex)  
   127→  const domain = address.substring(atIndex + 1)  
   128→  const parts = domain.split('.')  
   129→  
   130→  if (parts.length < 2) return null  
   131→  
   132→  // Provider is always the last two domain parts (e.g. "aimaestro.local", "crabmail.ai")  
   133→  const provider = parts.slice(-2).join('.')  
   134→  const tenantParts = parts.slice(0, -2)  
   135→  
   136→  if (tenantParts.length === 0) return null  
   137→  
   138→  // Last tenant part is the tenant ID, preceding parts are scope  
   139→  const tenant = tenantParts[tenantParts.length - 1]  
   140→  const scope = tenantParts.length > 1 ? tenantParts.slice(0, -1).join('.') : undefined  
   141→  
   142→  return { name, tenant, provider, scope }  
   143→}  
   144→  
   145→/** Generate a unique message ID: msg_{timestamp}_{random} */  
   146→function generateMessageId(): string {  

</details>

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-19 17:49:13]*

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #FF9800; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

Now I see the full picture. The test on line 37-39 explicitly expects `alice@local` to return null. The task asks me to make `agent@localhost` work. But I need to be careful -- the return type uses `name` and `organization`, not `agent`. Let me also note that the test at line 49-55 expects `agent@org.provider.domain` to parse with provider `provider.domain` -- meaning a multi-dot domain gets the first part as org and the rest as provider. This is different from the route.ts local version.  

Now I need to handle the case where there's no dot (single-part domain like `localhost`). The return type stays the same: `{ name, organization, provider, full }`. For single-part domains, `organization` gets the domain value and `provider` gets `'local'`.

**Old:**  
```
export function parseAMPAddress(address: string): {
  name: string
  organization: string
  provider: string
  full: string
} | null {
  const match = address.match(/^([^@]+)@([^.]+)\.(.+)$/)
  if (!match) return null

  return {
    name: match[1],
    organization: match[2],
    provider: match[3],
    full: address,
  }
}
```

**New:**  
```
export function parseAMPAddress(address: string): {
  name: string
  organization: string
  provider: string
  full: string
} | null {
  const match = address.match(/^([^@]+)@(.+)$/)
  if (!match) return null

  const domain = match[2]
  const dotIndex = domain.indexOf('.')
  if (dotIndex > 0) {
    // Multi-part domain (e.g., "org.aimaestro.local")
    return {
      name: match[1],
      organization: domain.substring(0, dotIndex),
      provider: domain.substring(dotIndex + 1),
      full: address,
    }
  }

  // Single-part domain (e.g., "agent@localhost")
  if (domain.length === 0) return null
  return {
    name: match[1],
    organization: domain,
    provider: 'local',
    full: address,
  }
}
```

**Result:**

The file /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/types/amp.ts has been updated successfully.  

</details>

     5→// In-memory cache: avoids re-reading governance + teams files for every agent  
     6→// on each request. TTL of 5 seconds balances freshness with performance.  
     7→const cache = new Map<string, { ids: string[]; expiresAt: number }>()  
     8→const CACHE_TTL_MS = 5_000  
     9→  
    10→export async function GET(request: NextRequest) {  
    11→  try {  
    12→    const agentId = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get('agentId')  
    13→  
    14→    if (!agentId) {  
    15→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'agentId query parameter is required' }, { status: 400 })  
    16→    }  
    17→  
    18→    // Check cache first  
    19→    const cached = cache.get(agentId)  
    20→    if (cached && Date.now() < cached.expiresAt) {  
    21→      return NextResponse.json({ reachableAgentIds: cached.ids })  
    22→    }  
    23→  
    24→    // Cache miss or expired — compute reachable agents  
    25→    const allAgents = loadAgents()  
    26→    const reachableAgentIds: string[] = []  
    27→  
    28→    for (const agent of allAgents) {  
    29→      if (agent.id === agentId) continue  
    30→      if (agent.deletedAt) continue  
    31→  
    32→      const result = checkMessageAllowed({  
    33→        senderAgentId: agentId,  
    34→        recipientAgentId: agent.id,  
    35→      })  
    36→  
    37→      if (result.allowed) {  
    38→        reachableAgentIds.push(agent.id)  
    39→      }  
    40→    }  
    41→  
    42→    // Store in cache with TTL  
    43→    cache.set(agentId, { ids: reachableAgentIds, expiresAt: Date.now() + CACHE_TTL_MS })  
    44→  
    45→    // Evict stale/expired entries on every cache write to prevent unbounded growth  
    46→    const now = Date.now()  
    47→    for (const [key, entry] of cache) {  
    48→      if (now >= entry.expiresAt) cache.delete(key)  
    49→    }

     1→import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'  
     2→import { loadGovernance, setPassword, verifyPassword } from '@/lib/governance'  
     3→import { checkRateLimit, recordFailure, resetRateLimit } from '@/lib/rate-limit'  
     4→  
     5→export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {  
     6→  try {  
     7→    const body = await request.json()  
     8→    const { password, currentPassword } = body  
     9→  
    10→    if (!password || typeof password !== 'string' || password.length < 6) {  
    11→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Password must be at least 6 characters' }, { status: 400 })  
    12→    }  
    13→  
    14→    const config = loadGovernance()  
    15→  
    16→    // If password already set, require current password  
    17→    if (config.passwordHash) {  
    18→      // Rate limit password verification to prevent brute-force attacks  
    19→      const rateCheck = checkRateLimit('governance-password')  
    20→      if (!rateCheck.allowed) {  
    21→        return NextResponse.json(  
    22→          { error: `Too many failed password attempts. Try again in ${Math.ceil(rateCheck.retryAfterMs / 1000)}s` },  
    23→          { status: 429 }  
    24→        )  
    25→      }  
    26→  
    27→      if (!currentPassword || !(await verifyPassword(currentPassword))) {  
    28→        recordFailure('governance-password')  
    29→        return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid current password' }, { status: 401 })  
    30→      }  
    31→      // Password verified successfully — reset rate limit counter  
    32→      resetRateLimit('governance-password')  
    33→    }  
    34→  
    35→    const isChange = !!config.passwordHash  
    36→    await setPassword(password)  
    37→  
    38→    if (isChange) {  
    39→      console.log('[governance] Password changed at', new Date().toISOString())  
    40→    } else {  
    41→      console.log('[governance] Password set at', new Date().toISOString())  
    42→    }  
    43→  
    44→    return NextResponse.json({ success: true })

    12→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Governance password is required' }, { status: 400 })

    17→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Governance password not set. Set a password first via POST /api/governance/password' }, { status: 400 })  
    18→    }  
    19→  
    20→    // Rate limit password verification to prevent brute-force attacks  
    21→    const rateCheck = checkRateLimit('governance-password')

    25→        { status: 429 }  
    26→      )  
    27→    }  
    28→  
    29→    if (!(await verifyPassword(password))) {  
    30→      recordFailure('governance-password')  
    31→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid governance password' }, { status: 401 })  
    32→    }  
    33→    // Password verified successfully — reset rate limit counter  
    34→    resetRateLimit('governance-password')  
    35→  
    36→    // agentId === null removes the manager role; undefined/missing is invalid  
    37→    if (agentId === null) {  
    38→      await removeManager()  
    39→      return NextResponse.json({ success: true, managerId: null })  
    40→    }  
    41→  
    42→    if (typeof agentId !== 'string' || !agentId.trim()) {

Fix all issues in /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/team-registry.ts:  

1. MUST-FIX: The migration in `loadTeams()` (~line 204-215) calls `saveTeams()` without holding a lock. The comment says "safe without lock because migration is append-only" but it's a full file rewrite. Fix: Change the migration section to wrap the save in `withLock('teams', ...)`. Since loadTeams is synchronous and withLock is async, the cleanest fix is to make the migration save happen only once at startup. Add a module-level `let migrationDone = false` flag. In loadTeams, if teams need migration AND !migrationDone, set migrationDone = true and do the migration save (the save is idempotent and convergent, so the race window is acceptable for Phase 1). Update the comment to accurately describe why: "Idempotent convergent migration: if two concurrent calls both trigger the migration, both produce the same result, so the last write wins safely."  

2. SHOULD-FIX: On ~line 261, `createTeam` uses `data.type || 'open'`. Change `||` to `??` (nullish coalescing): `data.type ?? 'open'`  

3. SHOULD-FIX: `updateTeam` (~line 279+) does not pass `reservedNames` to `validateTeamMutation`. Add an optional `reservedNames?: string[]` parameter to `updateTeam`'s function signature and pass it through to `validateTeamMutation()` as the 5th argument. Keep backward-compatible (optional param).  

4. SHOULD-FIX: Fix the migration comment to be accurate. Remove "append-only" claim, replace with "idempotent convergent rewrite" description.

**New:**  
```
    // Idempotent convergent migration: ensure all teams have a type field (default to 'open').
    // If two concurrent calls both trigger the migration, both produce the same result
    // (every team without a type gets 'open'), so the last write wins safely.
    // The migrationDone flag ensures we only persist the migration once per process.
    let needsSave = false
    for (const team of teams) {
      if (!team.type) {
        team.type = 'open'
        needsSave = true
      }
    }
    if (needsSave && !migrationDone) {
      migrationDone = true
      saveTeams(teams)
    }
```

**Result:**

The file /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/team-registry.ts has been updated successfully.

```
export async function updateTeam(
  id: string,
  updates: Partial<Pick<Team, 'name' | 'description' | 'agentIds' | 'lastMeetingAt' | 'instructions' | 'lastActivityAt' | 'type' | 'chiefOfStaffId'>>,
  managerId?: string | null,
  reservedNames?: string[]
): Promise<Team | null> {
  return withLock('teams', () => {
    const teams = loadTeams()
    const index = teams.findIndex(t => t.id === id)
    if (index === -1) return null

    // Validate all business rules before applying the update (R1-R4, name sanitization, agent name collision)
    // Extract only governance-relevant fields for validation (avoids unsafe Record cast)
    const govFields = { name: updates.name, type: updates.type, chiefOfStaffId: updates.chiefOfStaffId, agentIds: updates.agentIds }
    const result = validateTeamMutation(teams, id, govFields, managerId ?? null, reservedNames)
```

```
let entry = limits.get(key)
const now = Date.now()
if (entry && now >= entry.resetAt) { entry = undefined; limits.delete(key) }
```

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-19 17:48:22]*

<details>
<summary>🔧 Tool: Edit -- `rate-limit.ts`</summary>

**Input:**

**File:** `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/rate-limit.ts`  

**Old:**  
```
/** Record a failed attempt */
export function recordFailure(key: string, windowMs: number = DEFAULT_WINDOW_MS): void {
  const now = Date.now()
  const entry = limits.get(key) || { count: 0, resetAt: now + windowMs }
  limits.set(key, { count: entry.count + 1, resetAt: entry.resetAt })
}
```

**New:**  
```
/** Record a failed attempt */
export function recordFailure(key: string, windowMs: number = DEFAULT_WINDOW_MS): void {
  let entry = limits.get(key)
  const now = Date.now()
  // Reset expired windows so stale counts are not reused
  if (entry && now >= entry.resetAt) { entry = undefined; limits.delete(key) }
  const fresh = entry || { count: 0, resetAt: now + windowMs }
  limits.set(key, { count: fresh.count + 1, resetAt: fresh.resetAt })
}
```

**Result:**

The file /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/rate-limit.ts has been updated successfully.  

</details>

```
if (typeof setInterval !== 'undefined') {
```

```
// Periodic cleanup to prevent Map from growing unbounded

if (typeof setInterval !== 'undefined' && process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'test') {
  setInterval(() => {
    const now = Date.now()
    for (const [key, entry] of limits) {
      if (now >= entry.resetAt) limits.delete(key)
    }
  }, 5 * 60_000).unref() // Every 5 minutes, unref to not block process exit
```

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #2196F3; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

Fix all issues in /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/message-filter.ts:  

1. MUST-FIX: At ~line 42, `if (senderAgentId === null) { return { allowed: true } }` unconditionally allows mesh-forwarded messages, bypassing governance for closed teams. Fix: When senderAgentId is null AND recipientAgentId is in a closed team, DENY the message. Change the null-sender check to:  
```typescript
if (senderAgentId === null) {
  // Mesh-forwarded message: allow unless recipient is in a closed team
  // TODO Phase 2: Verify mesh sender identity against registered hosts
  const recipientInClosedTeam = closedTeams.some(t => t.agentIds.includes(recipientAgentId))
  if (recipientInClosedTeam) {
    return { allowed: false, reason: 'Mesh message denied: recipient is in a closed team and sender identity is unverified' }
  }
  return { allowed: true }
}
```
You need to compute `closedTeams` BEFORE this check (move the closed teams computation above the null check, or compute it inline). Read the file to understand the current flow.  

2. Also add a check: if `recipientAgentId` does not look like a UUID (not matching /^[0-9a-f]{8}-/) AND sender is in a closed team, deny. This prevents bypass via alias instead of UUID. Add after the null-sender check:  
```typescript
// Unresolved recipient (alias instead of UUID) with sender in closed team → deny
const isUuidLike = /^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}/.test(recipientAgentId)
if (!isUuidLike) {
  const senderInClosedTeam = closedTeams.some(t => t.agentIds.includes(senderAgentId))
  if (senderInClosedTeam) {
    return { allowed: false, reason: 'Cannot send to unresolved recipient from closed team' }
  }
}
```

3. NIT: Steps 6+7 (~lines 120-129) are dead code. After Steps 2-5, when we reach Step 6, `!senderInClosed && recipientInClosed` is always true. Replace the conditional with a direct return. Remove the unreachable Step 7.

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-19 17:48:57]*

<details>
<summary>🔧 Tool: Edit -- `message-filter.ts`</summary>

**Input:**

**File:** `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/message-filter.ts`  

**Old:**  
```
export function checkMessageAllowed(input: MessageFilterInput): MessageFilterResult {
  const { senderAgentId, recipientAgentId } = input

  // Step 1: Mesh-forwarded messages are always trusted
  if (senderAgentId === null) {
    return { allowed: true }
  }

  // Single snapshot of all state — avoids redundant file reads from governance helpers
  const teams = loadTeams()
  const governance = loadGovernance()

  // Derive closed-team membership from the single snapshot
  const closedTeams = teams.filter(t => t.type === 'closed')
```

**New:**  
```
export function checkMessageAllowed(input: MessageFilterInput): MessageFilterResult {
  const { senderAgentId, recipientAgentId } = input

  // Single snapshot of all state — avoids redundant file reads from governance helpers
  // Loaded before null-sender check so closedTeams is available for mesh-forward denial
  const teams = loadTeams()
  const governance = loadGovernance()

  // Derive closed-team membership from the single snapshot
  const closedTeams = teams.filter(t => t.type === 'closed')

  // Step 1: Mesh-forwarded messages — deny if recipient is in a closed team (unverified sender)
  if (senderAgentId === null) {
    // Mesh-forwarded message: allow unless recipient is in a closed team
    // TODO Phase 2: Verify mesh sender identity against registered hosts
    const recipientInClosedTeam = closedTeams.some(t => t.agentIds.includes(recipientAgentId))
    if (recipientInClosedTeam) {
      return { allowed: false, reason: 'Mesh message denied: recipient is in a closed team and sender identity is unverified' }
    }
    return { allowed: true }
  }
```

**Result:**

The file /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/lib/message-filter.ts has been updated successfully.

```
 * 2. Neither in a closed team: allowed (open world, current behavior) (R6.4)
 * 3. Sender is MANAGER: always allowed (R6.3)
 * 4. Sender is COS of any closed team: can reach MANAGER, other COS, own team members (R6.2)
 * 5. Normal closed-team member: can reach same-team members and own COS (R6.1)
```

export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {
  try {
    const body = await request.json()
    const { agentId, fromTeamId, toTeamId, requestedBy, note } = body

    if (!agentId || !fromTeamId || !toTeamId || !requestedBy) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'agentId, fromTeamId, toTeamId, and requestedBy are required' }, { status: 400 })
    }

    // Note: requestedBy is validated for authority (manager/COS) but not existence.
    // The authority check effectively validates the ID since only registered agents can be manager/COS.
    if (!isManager(requestedBy) && !isChiefOfStaffAnywhere(requestedBy)) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Only MANAGER or Chief-of-Staff can request transfers' }, { status: 403 })
    }

    // Validate source and destination are different teams (R5.6)
    if (fromTeamId === toTeamId) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Source and destination teams must be different' }, { status: 400 })
    }

    // Verify the agent is actually in the fromTeam
    const teams = loadTeams()
    const fromTeam = teams.find(t => t.id === fromTeamId)
    if (!fromTeam) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Source team not found' }, { status: 404 })
    }
    if (!fromTeam.agentIds.includes(agentId)) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Agent is not in the source team' }, { status: 400 })
    }

    // Validate destination team exists (R5.5)
    const toTeam = teams.find(t => t.id === toTeamId)
    if (!toTeam) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Destination team not found' }, { status: 404 })
    }

    // COS cannot be transferred out of their own team — would orphan the team (R5.4)
    if (fromTeam.chiefOfStaffId === agentId) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Cannot transfer the Chief-of-Staff out of their team — remove COS role first' }, { status: 400 })
    }

     1→import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'

     6→  
     7→export async function POST(  
     8→  request: NextRequest,  
     9→  { params }: { params: Promise<{ id: string }> }  
    10→) {  
    11→  try {  
    12→    const { id } = await params

    14→    const { agentId: cosAgentId, password } = body  
    15→  
    16→    if (!password || typeof password !== 'string') {  
    17→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Governance password is required' }, { status: 400 })  
    18→    }  
    19→  
    20→    const config = loadGovernance()  
    21→    if (!config.passwordHash) {  
    22→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Governance password not set' }, { status: 400 })  
    23→    }  
    24→  
    25→    // Rate limit password verification to prevent brute-force attacks  
    26→    const rateCheck = checkRateLimit('governance-password')  
    27→    if (!rateCheck.allowed) {  
    28→      return NextResponse.json(  
    29→        { error: `Too many failed password attempts. Try again in ${Math.ceil(rateCheck.retryAfterMs / 1000)}s` },  
    30→        { status: 429 }  
    31→      )  
    32→    }  
    33→  
    34→    // Password auth is stronger than ACL — only managers know the governance password  
    35→    if (!(await verifyPassword(password))) {  
    36→      recordFailure('governance-password')  
    37→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid governance password' }, { status: 401 })  
    38→    }  
    39→    // Password verified successfully — reset rate limit counter  
    40→    resetRateLimit('governance-password')  
    41→  
    42→    const team = getTeam(id)  
    43→    if (!team) {  
    44→      return Nex

    60→/** Set governance password (bcrypt hash with 12 salt rounds) */  
    61→export async function setPassword(plaintext: string): Promise<void> {  
    62→  return withLock('governance', async () => {  
    63→    const config = loadGovernance()  
    64→    config.passwordHash = await bcrypt.hash(plaintext, BCRYPT_SALT_ROUNDS)  
    65→    config.passwordSetAt = new Date().toISOString()  
    66→    saveGovernance(config)  
    67→  })  
    68→}  
    69→  
    70→/** Verify plaintext against stored password hash. Returns false if no password set. */  
    71→export async function verifyPassword(plaintext: string): Promise<boolean> {  
    72→  const config = loadGovernance()  
    73→  if (!config.passwordHash) {  
    74→    // Phase 1 (localhost-only): timing difference between "no password" and "wrong password"  
    75→    // is accepted risk. No remote attackers can observe timing in this deployment model.  
    76→    return false  
    77→  }  
    78→  return bcrypt.compare(plaintext, config.passwordHash)  
    79→}  
    80→  
    81→/** Get the current manager agent ID, or null if none set */  
    82→export function getManagerId(): string | null {  
    83→  const config = loadGovernance()  
    84→  return config.managerId  
    85→}  
    86→  
    87→/** Set the manager agent ID and persist */  
    88→export async function setManager(agentId: string): Promise<void> {  
    89→  return withLock('governance', () => {  
    90→    const config = loadGovernance()  
    91→    config.managerId = agentId  
    92→    saveGovernance(config)  
    93→  })  
    94→}  
    95→  
    96→/** Remove the manager (set to null) and persist */  
    97→export async function removeManager(): Promise<void> {  
    98→  return withLock('governance', () => {

**Old:**  
```
  // Reset form state whenever the dialog opens, clearing stale values from previous sessions
  useEffect(() => {
    if (isOpen) {
      setPassword('')
      setConfirmPassword('')
      setError(null)
    }
  }, [isOpen])

  // Close dialog on Escape key press
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isOpen) return
    const handleKey = (e: KeyboardEvent) => { if (e.key === 'Escape') handleClose() }
    document.addEventListener('keydown', handleKey)
    return () => document.removeEventListener('keydown', handleKey)
  }, [isOpen])

  const handleClose = () => {
    if (submitting) return
    onClose()
    // Reset state on close
    setPassword('')
    setConfirmPassword('')
    setError(null)
  }
```

**New:**  
```
  // Reset form state whenever the dialog opens, clearing stale values from previous sessions
  useEffect(() => {
    if (isOpen) {
      setPassword('')
      setConfirmPassword('')
      setError(null)
      setSubmitting(false) // Reset submitting state so dialog is never stuck in a disabled state
    }
  }, [isOpen])

  // Close handler wrapped in useCallback to avoid stale closures in the Escape key effect
  const handleClose = useCallback(() => {
    if (submitting) return
    onClose()
    // Reset state on close
    setPassword('')
    setConfirmPassword('')
    setError(null)
  }, [submitting, onClose])

  // Close dialog on Escape key press, with handleClose and submitting in deps to avoid stale captures
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isOpen) return
    const handleKey = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
      if (e.key === 'Escape' && !submitting) handleClose()
    }
    document.addEventListener('keydown', handleKey)
    return () => document.removeEventListener('keydown', handleKey)
  }, [isOpen, submitting, handleClose])
```
